linguas="ar as ast be be@latin bg bn bn_IN bs ca ca@valencia cs da de el en_GB en@shaw eo es et eu fa fi fr ga gl gu he hi hu id it ja kk kn ko ku lt lv mai mk ml mr ms nb ne nl nn oc or pa pl pt pt_BR ro ru si sk sl sq sr sr@latin sv ta te tg th tr ug uk vi zh_CN zh_HK zh_TW "; \

  dir=/tmp/vinagre/pkg/vinagre/usr/share/locale/$lang/LC_MESSAGES; \
  /bin/sh /tmp/vinagre/src/vinagre-3.18.1/build-aux/install-sh -d $dir; \
  if test -r $lang.gmo; then \
    /usr/bin/install -c -m 644 $lang.gmo $dir/vinagre.mo; \
    echo "installing $lang.gmo as $dir/vinagre.mo"; \
  else \
    /usr/bin/install -c -m 644 ./$lang.gmo $dir/vinagre.mo; \
    echo "installing ./$lang.gmo as" \
	 "$dir/vinagre.mo"; \
  fi; \
  if test -r $lang.gmo.m; then \
    /usr/bin/install -c -m 644 $lang.gmo.m $dir/vinagre.mo.m; \
    echo "installing $lang.gmo.m as $dir/vinagre.mo.m"; \
  else \
    if test -r ./$lang.gmo.m ; then \
      /usr/bin/install -c -m 644 ./$lang.gmo.m \
	$dir/vinagre.mo.m; \
      echo "installing ./$lang.gmo.m as" \
	   "$dir/vinagre.mo.m"; \
    else \
      true; \
    fi; \
  fi; \
done
